PRELIMINARY ROOT CAUSE: Engineers identified a recent configuration change to the Order Management System (OMS) which impacted the payment process. MITIGATION: Engineers reverted to the previous configuration, which has mitigated the issue. New customers should no longer be affected, and will be able to sign up for new Azure accounts. Customers renewing their account payment details should also be able to process now without issue. Any customer who experienced a failure when processing a payment will receive a direct message through their portal notifying them to retry this transaction. NEXT ACTION: Engineers will continue to investigate to establish full root cause, and update our deployment and testing methodologies to prevent future occurrences. \r\n[9/22/2016 12:26:31 PM] UTC - 影响总结：开始时间： 2016/09/22 03:44 CST 结束时间：2016/09/22 15:09 CST 部分中国区域的Azure在线支付客户在尝试登录或提交支付申请时可能会遇到问题。 初步调查结果：我们的工程师确认是最近的一次账单管理系统(OMS)的配置更新影响到了在线支付功能。 解决办法：我们的工程师通过将账单管理系统(OMS)的配置恢复到之前的设置解决了这一问题。客户提交新的支付申请时以及登录账户时不会再遇到此问题。客户在对账户重新进行支付时也不会再遇到此问题。所有在支付过程中遇到问题的客户都将会直接从管理门户上收到一条信息告知他们去重新提交支付申请。 下一步举措：我们的工程师将会继续从全方位调查此问题的根本原因，升级更新并测试其结果以保证未来不会再出现此类问题。 SUMMARY OF IMPACT: Between 03:44 and 15:05 CST on 22 Sept, 2016, a subset of customers encountered an error when attempting to sign up or submit payment for Azure China. Customers renewing their account payment details should also be able to process now without issue. Any customer who experienced a failure when processing a payment will receive a direct message through their portal notifying them to retry this transaction. NEXT ACTION: Engineers will continue to investigate to establish full root cause, and update our deployment and testing methodologies to prevent future occurrences. "
